class="elementor-spacer-inner"></div> </div> </div> </div> </div> </div> </div> </section> <div class="elementor-element elementor-element-8aac130 e-con-full e-flex e-con e-parent" data-id="8aac130" data-element_type="container" data-e-type="container"> <div class="elementor-element elementor-element-3889fd7 e-con-full e-flex e-con e-child" data-id="3889fd7" data-element_type="container" data-e-type="container"> <div class="elementor-element elementor-element-6398747 elementor-widget elementor-widget-heading" data-id="6398747" data-element_type="widget" data-e-type="widget" data-widget_type="heading.default"> <div class="elementor-widget-container"> <h2 class="elementor-heading-title elementor-size-default">Energy Hunter – HVAC - Chiller condenser protection</h2> </div> </div> <div class="elementor-element elementor-element-42ef99e elementor-widget elementor-widget-text-editor" data-id="42ef99e" data-element_type="widget" data-e-type="widget" data-widget_type="text-editor.default"> <div class="elementor-widget-container"> <p>The condenser of a chiller using open cooling tower water is prone to develop a layer of CaCO<sub>3</sub>. Rule of thumb in the industry is that a 1 mm coating of CaCO<sub>3</sub> inside the tubes, can mean 3°C higher condensation temperature of the refrigerant gas at the condenser. This equates to approximately 10% higher condensation pressure and higher electricity consumption of the compressor.</p> </div> </div> <div class="elementor-element elementor-element-7cb4be0 elementor-align-center elementor-widget elementor-widget-button" data-id="7cb4be0" data-element_type="widget" data-e-type="widget" data-widget_type="button.default"> <div class="elementor-widget-container"> <div class="elementor-button-wrapper"> <a class="elementor-button elementor-button-link elementor-size-sm" href="https://www.suryasankara.in/wp-content/uploads/2024/01/Chiller-condenser-protection-and-savings-with-AHRI_training-material_EN_HIRES.pdf"> <span class="elementor-button-content-wrapper">
									<span class="elementor-button-text">Application Sheet</span>
					</span> </a> </div> </div> </div> </div> <div class="elementor-element elementor-element-5ad191d e-con-full e-flex e-con e-child" data-id="5ad191d" data-element_type="container" data-e-type="container"> <div class="elementor-element elementor-element-fd8d2df elementor-widget elementor-widget-heading" data-id="fd8d2df" data-element_type="widget" data-e-type="widget" data-widget_type="heading.default"> <div class="elementor-widget-container"> <h2 class="elementor-heading-title elementor-size-default">Energy Hunter – Utilities - ​​​​​​​Heat recovery from air compressors</h2> </div> </div> <div class="elementor-element elementor-element-7aa0ece elementor-widget elementor-widget-text-editor" data-id="7aa0ece" data-element_type="widget" data-e-type="widget" data-widget_type="text-editor.default"> <div class="elementor-widget-container"> <p>72% is the conversion of electricity to waste heat with air compressors. Compressed air and lubricating oil are often cooled with in built heat exchangers, releasing the heat to the atmosphere. Cooling the air also helps the dryer run effectively, reducing moisture content for critical air equipment.</p> </div> </div> <div class="elementor-element elementor-element-5d2bbb9 elementor-align-center elementor-widget elementor-widget-button" data-id="5d2bbb9" data-element_type="widget" data-e-type="widget" data-widget_type="button.default"> <div class="elementor-widget-container"> <div class="elementor-button-wrapper"> <a class="elementor-button elementor-button-link elementor-size-sm" href="https://www.suryasankara.in/wp-content/uploads/2024/01/Heat-recovery-from-air-compressors_training-material_EN_HIRES.pdf"> <span class="elementor-button-content-wrapper">
									<span class="elementor-button-text">Application Sheet</span>
					</span> </a> </div> </div> </div> </div> <div class="elementor-element elementor-element-140934e e-con-full e-flex e-con e-child" data-id="140934e" data-element_type="container" data-e-type="container"> <div class="elementor-element elementor-element-d951a7d elementor-widget elementor-widget-heading" data-id="d951a7d" data-element_type="widget" data-e-type="widget" data-widget_type="heading.default"> <div class="elementor-widget-container"> <h2 class="elementor-heading-title elementor-size-default">Energy Hunter – Utilities - Cooling tower interchanger​​​​​​​</h2> </div> </div> <div class="elementor-element elementor-element-5a1622e elementor-widget elementor-widget-text-editor" data-id="5a1622e" data-element_type="widget" data-e-type="widget" data-widget_type="text-editor.default"> <div class="elementor-widget-container"> <p>Plant cooling equipment protection from open cooling tower mineral deposits CaCO<sub>3</sub> and Chloride ions, minimum fouling from debris. Savings are in maintenance-free operation of plant equipment, lower pumping costs avoiding pipe diameter reduction and replacement of corroded equipment.</p> </div> </div> <div class="elementor-element elementor-element-9bde0b1 elementor-align-center elementor-widget elementor-widget-button" data-id="9bde0b1" data-element_type="widget" data-e-type="widget" data-widget_type="button.default"> <div class="elementor-widget-container"> <div class="elementor-button-wrapper"> <a class="elementor-button elementor-button-link elementor-size-sm" href="https://www.suryasankara.in/wp-content/uploads/2024/01/Cooling-tower-interchanger_training-material_EN_HIRES.pdf"> <span class="elementor-button-content-wrapper">
									<span class="elementor-button-text">Application Sheet</span>
					</span> </a> </div> </div> </div> </div> </div> <div class="elementor-element elementor-element-2a02133 e-con-full e-flex e-con e-parent" data-id="2a02133" data-element_type="container" data-e-type="container"> <div class="elementor-element elementor-element-3356dc6 e-con-full e-flex e-con e-child" data-id="3356dc6" data-element_type="container" data-e-type="container"> <div class="elementor-element elementor-element-476a0d6 elementor-widget elementor-widget-heading" data-id="476a0d6" data-element_type="widget" data-e-type="widget" data-widget_type="heading.default"> <div class="elementor-widget-container"> <h2 class="elementor-heading-title elementor-size-default">Energy Hunter – HVAC - AHRI performance certification</h2> </div> </div> <div class="elementor-element elementor-element-f8f1aab elementor-widget elementor-widget-text-editor" data-id="f8f1aab" data-element_type="widget" data-e-type="widget" data-widget_type="text-editor.default"> <div class="elementor-widget-container"> <p>Can you accurately measure 0.5°C? What happens to the operation of the chiller if the installed pressure breaker gasketed plate heat exchanger under performs by 0.5 °C? Lower evaporation temperatures lead to higher lift with the chiller compressor and increasing electricity consumption of up to 3%. Installing Performance Certified gasketed plate heat exchangers provides a payback period of under three years.</p> </div> </div> <div class="elementor-element elementor-element-a528cc8 elementor-align-center elementor-widget elementor-widget-button" data-id="a528cc8" data-element_type="widget" data-e-type="widget" data-widget_type="button.default"> <div class="elementor-widget-container"> <div class="elementor-button-wrapper"> <a class="elementor-button elementor-button-link elementor-size-sm" href="https://www.suryasankara.in/wp-content/uploads/2024/01/AHRI-sustainable-high-rise_training-material_EN_HIRES.pdf"> <span class="elementor-button-content-wrapper">
									<span class="elementor-button-text">Application Sheet</span>
					</span> </a> </div> </div> </div> </div> <div class="elementor-element elementor-element-bf5d393 e-con-full e-flex e-con e-child" data-id="bf5d393" data-element_type="container" data-e-type="container"> <div class="elementor-element elementor-element-6daddb6 elementor-widget elementor-widget-heading" data-id="6daddb6" data-element_type="widget" data-e-type="widget" data-widget_type="heading.default"> <div class="elementor-widget-container"> <h2 class="elementor-heading-title elementor-size-default">Energy Hunter – Utilities - Heat recovery from warm wastewater</h2> </div> </div> <div class="elementor-element elementor-element-14dc763 elementor-widget elementor-widget-text-editor" data-id="14dc763" data-element_type="widget" data-e-type="widget" data-widget_type="text-editor.default"> <div class="elementor-widget-container"> <p>With Alfa Laval wide gap plate technology, heat recovery is efficient at the same time blockage free for wastewater containing &lt; 5 mm particles or fibres. Wastewater temperatures as low as 35°C and as low 10 m³ per hour can save 175 kilowatts (150,000 kCal/hr) with a payback period of less than six months, preheating the boiler feed water to 30°C.</p> </div> </div> <div class="elementor-element elementor-element-612d884 elementor-align-center elementor-widget elementor-widget-button" data-id="612d884" data-element_type="widget" data-e-type="widget" data-widget_type="button.default"> <div class="elementor-widget-container"> <div class="elementor-button-wrapper"> <a class="elementor-button elementor-button-link elementor-size-sm" href="https://www.suryasankara.in/wp-content/uploads/2024/01/Heat-recovery-from-warm-wastewater_training-material_EN_HIRES.pdf"> <span class="elementor-button-content-wrapper">
									<span class="elementor-button-text">Application Sheet</span>
					</span> </a> </div> </div> </div> </div> <div class="elementor-element elementor-element-e136415 e-con-full e-flex e-con e-child" data-id="e136415" data-element_type="container" data-e-type="container"> <div class="elementor-element elementor-element-88e8e7c elementor-widget elementor-widget-heading" data-id="88e8e7c" data-element_type="widget" data-e-type="widget" data-widget_type="heading.default"> <div class="elementor-widget-container"> <h2 class="elementor-heading-title elementor-size-default">Energy Hunter – Utilities - Shell-and-tube replacement</h2> </div> </div> <div class="elementor-element elementor-element-2e80820 elementor-widget elementor-widget-text-editor" data-id="2e80820" data-element_type="widget" data-e-type="widget" data-widget_type="text-editor.default"> <div class="elementor-widget-container"> <p>Based on the right channel type of gasketed plate heat exchanger and proportional heat surface area. Savings are with less footprint – including removal space for tube bundle, less hold up volume hence faster response times, easier and quicker maintenance and heat losses to the atmosphere from the shell-and-tube surface. </p> </div> </div> <div class="elementor-element elementor-element-b31ce46 elementor-align-center elementor-widget elementor-widget-button" data-id="b31ce46" data-element_type="widget" data-e-type="widget" data-widget_type="button.default"> <div class="elementor-widget-container"> <div class="elementor-button-wrapper"> <a class="elementor-button elementor-button-link elementor-size-sm" href="https://www.suryasankara.in/wp-content/uploads/2024/01/Shell-and-tube-replacement-with-only-dimensional-data_training-material_EN_HIRES.pdf"> <span class="elementor-button-content-wrapper">
									<span class="elementor-button-text">Application Sheet</span>
					</span> </a> </div> </div> </div> </div> </div> <div class="elementor-element elementor-element-36b4a44 e-con-full e-flex e-con e-parent" data-id="36b4a44" data-element_type="container" data-e-type="container"> <div class="elementor-element elementor-element-8c79d43 e-con-full e-flex e-con e-child" data-id="8c79d43" data-element_type="container" data-e-type="container"> <div class="elementor-element elementor-element-24c65d3 elementor-widget elementor-widget-heading" data-id="24c65d3" data-element_type="widget" data-e-type="widget" data-widget_type="heading.default"> <div class="elementor-widget-container"> <h2 class="elementor-heading-title elementor-size-default">Energy Hunter – HVAC - Free cooling with chiller bypass</h2> </div> </div> <div class="elementor-element elementor-element-c13bc2f elementor-widget elementor-widget-text-editor" data-id="c13bc2f" data-element_type="widget" data-e-type="widget" data-widget_type="text-editor.default"> <div class="elementor-widget-container"> <p>A chiller is one of the highest running cost equipment in many plants. Those with a water-cooled condenser can win in two ways with an Alfa Laval gasketed plate heat exchanger. One to protect the chiller from CaCO<sub>3</sub> coating on the tubes, saving electricity with lower condensing temperature and pressure and the other is by turning the chiller off up to 30 days per year, depending on the geographic location and the wet-bulb temperature. AHRI Performance Certification is vital as approach temperatures of 1°C are needed and who can measure 0.5°C!</p> </div> </div> <div class="elementor-element elementor-element-c46adf7 elementor-align-center elementor-widget elementor-widget-button" data-id="c46adf7" data-element_type="widget" data-e-type="widget" data-widget_type="button.default"> <div class="elementor-widget-container"> <div class="elementor-button-wrapper"> <a class="elementor-button elementor-button-link elementor-size-sm" href="https://www.suryasankara.in/wp-content/uploads/2024/01/Free-cooling-with-chiller-bypass_training-material_EN_HIRES.pdf"> <span class="elementor-button-content-wrapper">
									<span class="elementor-button-text">Application Sheet</span>
					</span> </a> </div> </div> </div> </div> <div class="elementor-element elementor-element-3864a7b e-con-full e-flex e-con e-child" data-id="3864a7b" data-element_type="container" data-e-type="container"> <div class="elementor-element elementor-element-5d17bc6 elementor-widget elementor-widget-heading" data-id="5d17bc6" data-element_type="widget" data-e-type="widget" data-widget_type="heading.default"> <div class="elementor-widget-container"> <h2 class="elementor-heading-title elementor-size-default">Energy Hunter – Utilities - Heat recovery from waste flash steam</h2> </div> </div> <div class="elementor-element elementor-element-4cc5034 elementor-widget elementor-widget-text-editor" data-id="4cc5034" data-element_type="widget" data-e-type="widget" data-widget_type="text-editor.default"> <div class="elementor-widget-container"> <p>All industries using steam as a heat source have problems with steam management. With a simple cyclone separator at the condensate collection point, flash steam can be condensed, heating water up to 80°C. Recovering 500 kg per hour of flash steam can save up to 5,000 Euro per month. The return on investment is less than 3-6 months.</p> </div> </div> <div class="elementor-element elementor-element-25d40a7 elementor-widget elementor-widget-spacer" data-id="25d40a7" data-element_type="widget" data-e-type="widget" data-widget_type="spacer.default"> <div class="elementor-widget-container"> <div class="elementor-spacer"> <div class="elementor-spacer-inner"></div> </div> </div> </div> <div class="elementor-element elementor-element-1d2d92d elementor-align-center elementor-widget elementor-widget-button" data-id="1d2d92d" data-element_type="widget" data-e-type="widget" data-widget_type="button.default"> <div class="elementor-widget-container"> <div class="elementor-button-wrapper"> <a class="elementor-button elementor-button-link elementor-size-sm" href="https://www.suryasankara.in/wp-content/uploads/2024/01/Heat-recovery-from-waste-flash-steam_training-material_EN_HIRES.pdf"> <span class="elementor-button-content-wrapper">
									<span class="elementor-button-text">Application Sheet</span>
					</span> </a> </div> </div> </div> </div> <div class="elementor-element elementor-element-003aafd e-con-full e-flex e-con e-child" data-id="003aafd" data-element_type="container" data-e-type="container"> <div class="elementor-element elementor-element-3d51c26 elementor-widget elementor-widget-heading" data-id="3d51c26" data-element_type="widget" data-e-type="widget" data-widget_type="heading.default"> <div class="elementor-widget-container"> <h2 class="elementor-heading-title elementor-size-default">Energy Hunter – Utilities - Air compressor heat exchanger replacement</h2> </div> </div> <div class="elementor-element elementor-element-a73273b elementor-widget elementor-widget-text-editor" data-id="a73273b" data-element_type="widget" data-e-type="widget" data-widget_type="text-editor.default"> <div class="elementor-widget-container"> <p>The in-built heat exchangers delivered with the air compressor, require the open cooling tower to be a well-maintained, regularly flushed and treated, to avoid accumulation of calcium carbonate and chloride ions. If not, the brazed plate heat exchanger or shell-and-tube, could fail and require urgent replacement. A gasketed plate heat exchanger can be offered as a solution, that is more durable, against the harmful effects of calcium carbonate and chloride ions. ​​​​​​​</p> </div> </div> <div class="elementor-element elementor-element-962fbdd elementor-widget elementor-widget-spacer" data-id="962fbdd" data-element_type="widget" data-e-type="widget" data-widget_type="spacer.default"> <div class="elementor-widget-container"> <div class="elementor-spacer"> <div class="elementor-spacer-inner"></div> </div> </div> </div> <div class="elementor-element elementor-element-9a5813d elementor-align-center elementor-widget elementor-widget-button" data-id="9a5813d" data-element_type="widget" data-e-type="widget" data-widget_type="button.default"> <div class="elementor-widget-container"> <div class="elementor-button-wrapper"> <a class="elementor-button elementor-button-link elementor-size-sm" href="https://www.suryasankara.in/wp-content/uploads/2024/01/Heat-recovery-from-air-compressors_training-material_EN_HIRES-1.pdf"> <span class="elementor-button-content-wrapper">
									<span class="elementor-button-text">Application Sheet</span>
					</span> </a> </div> </div> </div> </div> </div> <div class="elementor-element elementor-element-204790e e-con-full e-flex e-con e-parent" data-id="204790e" data-element_type="container" data-e-type="container"> <div class="elementor-element elementor-element-392401f e-con-full e-flex e-con e-child" data-id="392401f" data-element_type="container" data-e-type="container"> <div class="elementor-element elementor-element-5266edd elementor-widget elementor-widget-heading" data-id="5266edd" data-element_type="widget" data-e-type="widget" data-widget_type="heading.default"> <div class="elementor-widget-container"> <h2 class="elementor-heading-title elementor-size-default">Energy Hunter – HVAC - Energy savings in ammonia chillers and heat pumps</h2> </div> </div> <div class="elementor-element elementor-element-eff2e0f elementor-widget elementor-widget-text-editor" data-id="eff2e0f" data-element_type="widget" data-e-type="widget" data-widget_type="text-editor.default"> <div class="elementor-widget-container"> <p>The condenser and evaporator of the chiller can either be of an air heat exchanger type or be cooled/heated by e.g. glycol, brine or water. By utilizing the later technology, the refrigerant charge can be kept to a minimum and the complete refrigeration system can be placed in one machine room connected to air coolers, energy wells, dry-coolers through secondary systems using a less sensitive media such as water, glycol or even CO<sub>2</sub>.​​​​​​​</p> </div> </div> <div class="elementor-element elementor-element-808ce24 elementor-align-center elementor-widget elementor-widget-button" data-id="808ce24" data-element_type="widget" data-e-type="widget" data-widget_type="button.default"> <div class="elementor-widget-container"> <div class="elementor-button-wrapper"> <a class="elementor-button elementor-button-link elementor-size-sm" href="https://www.suryasankara.in/wp-content/uploads/2024/01/Energy-savings-in-chiller-heat-pumps-with-PHEs_training-material_EN_HIRES.pdf"> <span class="elementor-button-content-wrapper">
									<span class="elementor-button-text">Application Sheet</span>
					</span> </a> </div> </div> </div> </div> <div class="elementor-element elementor-element-5e25223 e-con-full e-flex e-con e-child" data-id="5e25223" data-element_type="container" data-e-type="container"> <div class="elementor-element elementor-element-4c9ded6 elementor-widget elementor-widget-heading" data-id="4c9ded6" data-element_type="widget" data-e-type="widget" data-widget_type="heading.default"> <div class="elementor-widget-container"> <h2 class="elementor-heading-title elementor-size-default">Energy Hunter – Utilities - Heat recovery from waste flash steam</h2> </div> </div> <div class="elementor-element elementor-element-85e7772 elementor-widget elementor-widget-text-editor" data-id="85e7772" data-element_type="widget" data-e-type="widget" data-widget_type="text-editor.default"> <div class="elementor-widget-container"> <p>All industries using steam as a heat source have problems with steam management. With a simple cyclone separator at the condensate collection point, flash steam can be condensed, heating water up to 80°C. Recovering 500 kg per hour of flash steam can save up to 5,000 Euro per month. The return on investment is less than 3-6 months.</p> </div> </div> <div class="elementor-element elementor-element-04a9542 elementor-widget elementor-widget-spacer" data-id="04a9542" data-element_type="widget" data-e-type="widget" data-widget_type="spacer.default"> <div class="elementor-widget-container"> <div class="elementor-spacer"> <div class="elementor-spacer-inner"></div> </div> </div> </div> <div class="elementor-element elementor-element-a3b55ad elementor-align-center elementor-widget elementor-widget-button" data-id="a3b55ad" data-element_type="widget" data-e-type="widget" data-widget_type="button.default"> <div class="elementor-widget-container"> <div class="elementor-button-wrapper"> <a class="elementor-button elementor-button-link elementor-size-sm" href="https://www.suryasankara.in/wp-content/uploads/2024/01/Heat-recovery-from-waste-flash-steam_training-material_EN_HIRES.pdf"> <span class="elementor-button-content-wrapper">
									<span class="elementor-button-text">Application Sheet</span>
					</span> </a> </div> </div> </div> </div> <div class="elementor-element elementor-element-31037e2 e-con-full e-flex e-con e-child" data-id="31037e2" data-element_type="container" data-e-type="container"> <div class="elementor-element elementor-element-44a4cda elementor-widget elementor-widget-heading" data-id="44a4cda" data-element_type="widget" data-e-type="widget" data-widget_type="heading.default"> <div class="elementor-widget-container"> <h2 class="elementor-heading-title elementor-size-default">Energy Hunter – Utilities - Air compressor heat exchanger replacement</h2> </div> </div> <div class="elementor-element elementor-element-6815a03 elementor-widget elementor-widget-text-editor" data-id="6815a03" data-element_type="widget" data-e-type="widget" data-widget_type="text-editor.default"> <div class="elementor-widget-container"> <p>The in-built heat exchangers delivered with the air compressor, require the open cooling tower to be a well-maintained, regularly flushed and treated, to avoid accumulation of calcium carbonate and chloride ions. If not, the brazed plate heat exchanger or shell-and-tube, could fail and require urgent replacement. A gasketed plate heat exchanger can be offered as a solution, that is more durable, against the harmful effects of calcium carbonate and chloride ions. ​​​​​​​</p> </div> </div> <div class="elementor-element elementor-element-c779b3d elementor-align-center elementor-widget elementor-widget-button" data-id="c779b3d" data-element_type="widget" data-e-type="widget" data-widget_type="button.default"> <div class="elementor-widget-container"> <div class="elementor-button-wrapper"> <a class="elementor-button elementor-button-link elementor-size-sm" href="https://www.suryasankara.in/wp-content/uploads/2024/01/Heat-recovery-from-air-compressors_training-material_EN_HIRES-1.pdf"> <span class="elementor-button-content-wrapper">
									<span class="elementor-button-text">Application Sheet</span>
					</span> </a> </div> </div> </div> </div> </div> <div class="elementor-element elementor-element-ac64d7b e-con-full e-flex e-con e-parent" data-id="ac64d7b" data-element_type="container" data-e-type="container"> <div class="elementor-element elementor-element-54216c7 e-con-full e-flex e-con e-child" data-id="54216c7" data-element_type="container" data-e-type="container"> </div> <div class="elementor-element elementor-element-89c5c49 e-con-full e-flex e-con e-child" data-id="89c5c49" data-element_type="container" data-e-type="container"> <div class="elementor-element elementor-element-480ecc4 elementor-widget elementor-widget-heading" data-id="480ecc4" data-element_type="widget" data-e-type="widget" data-widget_type="heading.default"> <div class="elementor-widget-container"> <h2 class="elementor-heading-title elementor-size-default">Energy Hunter – Utilities - Boiler protection</h2> </div> </div> <div class="elementor-element elementor-element-54da667 elementor-widget elementor-widget-text-editor" data-id="54da667" data-element_type="widget" data-e-type="widget" data-widget_type="text-editor.default"> <div class="elementor-widget-container"> <p>Especially for retrofit applications, the building circuit can contain debris, mud, CaCO<sub>3</sub> and oxygenated water. The CaCO<sub>3</sub> can bake at 300°C plus fuel temperatures and with thermal expansion/contraction crack the boiler’s heater. Two identical buildings located side by side, one with gasketed plate heat exchanger protection and the other without, has fuel costs 30% less, as with protection, the boiler heater does not have a coating of CaCO<sub>3</sub>.</p> </div> </div> <div class="elementor-element elementor-element-3851beb elementor-align-center elementor-widget elementor-widget-button" data-id="3851beb" data-element_type="widget" data-e-type="widget" data-widget_type="button.default"> <div class="elementor-widget-container"> <div class="elementor-button-wrapper"> <a class="elementor-button elementor-button-link elementor-size-sm" href="https://www.suryasankara.in/wp-content/uploads/2024/01/Boiler-protection-with-GPHEs_training-material_EN_HIRES.pdf"> <span class="elementor-button-content-wrapper">
									<span class="elementor-button-text">Application Sheet</span>
					</span> </a> </div> </div> </div> </div> <div class="elementor-element elementor-element-fd4a128 e-con-full e-flex e-con e-child" data-id="fd4a128" data-element_type="container" data-e-type="container"> </div> </div> <div class="elementor-element elementor-element-9d31200 e-con-full e-flex e-con e-parent" data-id="9d31200" data-element_type="container" data-e-type="container"> <div class="elementor-element elementor-element-ce510d0 e-con-full e-flex e-con e-child" data-id="ce510d0" data-element_type="container" data-e-type="container"> </div> <div class="elementor-element elementor-element-18a29a9 e-con-full e-flex e-con e-child" data-id="18a29a9" data-element_type="container" data-e-type="container"> <div class="elementor-element elementor-element-5603b13 elementor-widget elementor-widget-heading" data-id="5603b13" data-element_type="widget" data-e-type="widget" data-widget_type="heading.default"> <div class="elementor-widget-container"> <h2 class="elementor-heading-title elementor-size-default">Energy Hunter – Utilities - Heat recovery from open cooling tower</h2> </div> </div> <div class="elementor-element elementor-element-8c3759a elementor-widget elementor-widget-text-editor" data-id="8c3759a" data-element_type="widget" data-e-type="widget" data-widget_type="text-editor.default"> <div class="elementor-widget-container"> <p>This is exceptionally beneficial where heating and cooling takes place at the same plant. Typically for preheating boiler feed water close as 2°C to cooling tower return. Savings are in increased cooling tower capacity, less fuel costs for boiler operation (almost half) and less evaporation of water at the tower, hence saving water.​​​​​​​</p> </div> </div> <div class="elementor-element elementor-element-48ae70b elementor-align-center elementor-widget elementor-widget-button" data-id="48ae70b" data-element_type="widget" data-e-type="widget" data-widget_type="button.default"> <div class="elementor-widget-container"> <div class="elementor-button-wrapper"> <a class="elementor-button elementor-button-link elementor-size-sm" href="https://www.suryasankara.in/wp-content/uploads/2024/01/Heat-recovery-from-open-cooling-tower_training-material_EN_HIRES.pdf"> <span class="elementor-button-content-wrapper">
									<span class="elementor-button-text">Application Sheet</span>
					</span> </a> </div> </div> </div> </div> <div class="elementor-element elementor-element-bb5546a e-con-full e-flex e-con e-child" data-id="bb5546a" data-element_type="container"
